if (!is_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') != '13d0fc32d84a51e6a928f63f0a8d9a30fb25843e') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') !== '13d0fc32d84a51e6a928f63f0a8d9a30fb25843e') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') !== 'f7362a562828bd79d5ac81e0b57205df241a5ec4') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') !== '13d0fc32d84a51e6a928f63f0a8d9a30fb25843e') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
		}
	}
}

	if (@sha1_file('dev/vendor_update.sh') !== '86e78957404ea97c4ee3501ed94554fc9245a91c') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/vendor_update.sh') !== '3546840d1d4d009936ceb1d400696d75a533a192') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/vendor_update.sh');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/vendor_update.sh');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/vendor_update.sh')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/vendor_update.sh', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/vendor_update.sh') !== '86e78957404ea97c4ee3501ed94554fc9245a91c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/vendor_update.sh');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') != 'd157dca5c54d78de6d39597115756f20fc111fd6') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'd157dca5c54d78de6d39597115756f20fc111fd6') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '2283561d0c889f351e89ea3b7d079ccdf2cbbff2') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'd157dca5c54d78de6d39597115756f20fc111fd6') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}
